1 # This table comes from MS CP950 table posted on unicode.org webpage
    2 # with the modifications of 
    3 #
    4 # (1)removed single byte entries 
    5 #      0x00 - 0x7f
    6 # (2)removed DBCS lead byte entries 
    7 #      0x80 - 0xff  
    8 # (3)added EUDC entries.
    9 #      0xFA40 - 0xFEFE  U+E000 - U+E310  
   10 #      0x8E40 - 0xA0FE  U+E311 - U+EEB7  
   11 #      0x8140 - 0x8DFE  U+EEB8 - U+F6B0  
   12 #      0xC6A1 - 0xC8FE  U+F6B1 - U+F848  
   13 # (4)roundtrip mapping conflicts
   14 #    0xF9FA -> u256D -> 0xA27E 
   15 #    0xF9FB -> u256E -> 0xA2A1 
   16 #    0xF9FC -> u2570 -> 0xA2A2 
   17 #    0xF9FD -> u256F -> 0xA2A3 
   18 #    0xA2CC -> u5341 -> 0xA451 
   19 #    0xA2CE -> u5345 -> 0xA4CA  
   20 #    0xF9F9 -> u2550 -> 0xA2A4
   21 #    0xF9E9 -> u255E -> 0xA2A5	
   22 #    0xF9EA -> u256A -> 0xA2A6	
   23 #    0xF9EB -> u2561 -> 0xA2A7
   24 #
   25 # Column #1 is the cp950 code (in hex)
   26 # Column #2 is the Unicode (in hex as 0xXXXX)
   27 # Column #3 is the Unicode name (follows a comment sign, '#')
   28 #
